Suzhou

Public Security Bureau Again Captures Communists: Since capturing Song Qin, a communist who was distributing leaflets along the Xiao Jia Xiang Kou on the 7th of last month, the Public Security Bureau has successively captured as many as twenty-four people, including Yao Ji An and Wang Chun Tao. Except for twelve of them who were released on bail after being found to have no involvement, the Third Public Security Bureau, on the previous day (the first), received a secret order to, together with Chen Zhi Jun of the Party Rectification Committee, go to No. 57, Bei Hao Nong and capture Duan Ming Huan and Hu Xing, two communists. They also found in their room a copy of "Twelve Letters to the People," a copy of "Armed Riot Order," a scrapbook of military news cut and pasted from newspapers, and a "Survey Form of Garrison, Police, and Merchant Corps' Firearms in Suzhou." There was also a plan to use hand-held grenades to carry out riots during the upcoming Double Tenth Festival, which included the phrase "first rob the East Market to collect money." They were arrested together with the landlord, Lu Gen Lin, and a suspect, Liu Ming Lun, and taken to the bureau. After interrogation by Director Zou, a team was immediately dispatched to continue searching for remaining accomplices in various places. The government has decided to declare a special curfew in Suzhou during the Double Tenth Festival, cancel the lantern parade, and, starting yesterday (the 2nd), the Public Security Bureau has added Li Ya Dong (originally held by Fan Zhong Ying) to inspect mail, and Wang Shi Yi (originally held by Tang Tian Qiu) to inspect telegrams.

Busy Collecting 19th Year Barge Tax: The Wuxian Finance Bureau is preparing to collect the silver for the 19th year upper barge tax. The Wuxian territory floral household registers have been successively completed and collection has already begun on the previous day (the first). The upper barge tax should be levied at a rate of 3 yuan, 0 jiao, 9 fen, 2 li, and 2 and a half hao of foreign currency for each tael, including both the principal and supplementary taxes. It is limited to be paid at the counter within two months.

Foreign Ships Not Responsible for Compensation: The Shanghai Meifu Company's No. 11 gasoline ship was previously robbed by lake bandits in the Shi Ren Miao area of Taihu Lake, and a British employee was shot and injured. The US Consul General in Shanghai, Ke Ning Han, repeatedly sent letters to the Wuxian County Government, demanding compensation of over 500 yuan in foreign currency. Magistrate Huang immediately submitted the letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for review. Yesterday, he received instructions roughly stating that, according to international practice, in such cases, local government offices only need to strictly investigate and arrest the stolen goods and are not responsible for compensation. The request should be rejected.

Salt City Magistrate Accused: Du Wei, the magistrate of Yancheng County, was recently accused by You Bo Tao in a petition to the High Court, accusing Magistrate Du of illegally arresting people from afar and coercing confessions. He requested relief. After receiving the petition, the High Court Prosecutor's Office has already approved the case yesterday, ordering Qian Ji Long, the chief prosecutor of the First High Court Branch, to investigate and handle it.

Wuxi

Lake Bandits Discovered in Hudai Town: Hudai Town, in the 17th district (Fuan Township) of this county, is located on the edge of Taihu Lake and has always been a place where lake bandits appear. The town's businesses are prosperous and the residents are densely populated. In the previous year, it was looted by a large gang of lake bandits, causing great losses. Unexpectedly, yesterday, a large gang of lake bandits came to the town again, disguised as villagers, plotting to repeat their actions. The general residents were greatly panicked. Seeing this, the town's merchant corps also stepped up their defenses, fearing that their strength was weak, they specially sent someone to report to the district office in Zhangsheli, which was forwarded to the Public Security Bureau to send a team to assist. After receiving the report, Director Xu immediately dispatched Miao Wencheng, the deputy captain of the detective team, leading four detectives, carrying handguns, to go to the countryside for investigation. After returning to report, a team will be sent to suppress them.

Divination and Astrology Asked to Postpone the Ban: Divination and astrology have long been ordered to be banned, and all practitioners are required to change their profession after three months. Dozens of diviners and astrologers residing in this county, including Liu Fu Ren, jointly submitted a petition to the county government yesterday, roughly stating that they set up stalls, use character divination as a name, and make a living by writing letters for people, and that all prohibited items have been discarded. They requested consideration of their poverty and a postponement of the ban to allow them to gradually change their profession to maintain their livelihood.

Yixing Bandit Police and Water Police Defense: Yixing is located on the edge of Taihu Lake, and lake bandits often cause trouble. Previously, County Magistrate Sun Gong Qi telegraphed the Second District of the Wuxi Water Police, requesting them to send police to assist in the suppression. After receiving the telegram, District Chief Mao Mu Jun immediately telegraphed Huang Cheng Ji, the captain of the Ninth Team stationed in Yixing, to quickly cooperate with the operation. However, recently the lake bandits have become increasingly rampant, and the situation is extremely dangerous. District Chief Mao repeatedly received urgent telegrams from the Yixing County Government. Yesterday, he specially ordered the Bao Su warship to go to suppress the bandits, and telegraphed the Ninth Team stationed in Yixing to immediately open the Zhou Tie Qiao Sha Tang Feng, and jointly encircle and suppress the bandits with the fleet and the land army and police. He also telegraphed Sun County Magistrate of Yixing to check. In addition, the Water Police Eighth Team stationed in Dongshan, recently because the South Taihu Lake is close to Dongshan, and the lake bandits use Ganglu as their lair, and recently there are hundreds of people gathering together to cause trouble, the defense is extremely important. However, Xishan is located around the lake without Ganglu, and the defense cannot be ignored. He specially telegraphed District Chief Mao to send a warship to drag a gunboat to patrol Xishan every day, in order to keep abreast of the news and consolidate the defense. District Chief Mao approved the telegram and ordered Yang Wen Kui, the captain of the Luo Ping warship, to lead the warship to go and patrol with the eighth team's patrol boats to jointly defend and suppress the bandits in order to maintain security.

Winter Barge Tax Collection of Education Land Donation: The county government, due to the exhaustion of education funds and the inability to raise funds, previously submitted opinions from Lu Ren Shou, the director of the Education Bureau, to the county political conference. Within the prescribed limit, education land donation was collected under the winter barge tax. After the discussion and resolution, it was submitted to the Finance and Education Departments by the county, and then to the provincial government. The provincial government meeting added amendments, approving 3 jiao, 8 fen, 9 li of silver per shi of barge rice. It was immediately resolved and approved, and the Finance and Education Departments were ordered to comply. Yesterday, the county government received instructions from the Finance Department, and immediately instructed the Finance Bureau to comply.

Changzhou

Hutangqiao Bone Cargo Ship Robbed: A bone cargo ship was docked at Hutangqiao, south of Wuyi, the other day. The two ship owners, Tang Quan Fu and Tang Xi Bao, were sleeping at night when more than ten bandits came, each holding guns and flashlights, with white cloths tied around their heads. They boarded the ship and robbed 162 yuan in silver dollars and clothes. After the incident, the nearby police station learned about it and reported it to the Public Security Bureau on the first day, which was forwarded to the county to order the arrest.

Dachengqiao Bandits Threw Letters of Intimidation: Dachengqiao, located at the junction of Wuxi and Danyang, has an oil mill. In front of Chenmen one morning, a threatening letter suddenly appeared, with a brick placed on top. When the letter was opened, it stated that the shops and residents of the town should provide 6,000 yuan in foreign currency and deliver it to Bababaqiao in Yangzhou within three days, otherwise the entire town would be looted. The residents and shops in the town were extremely panicked and were on alert.

Nantong

Wounded Soldiers Set Off for Pukou: Over 1,100 wounded soldiers from the 31st Rear Hospital are currently being handled for discharge by Shao Za Han and Huang Zhuo Jie, who were assigned by the Commander-in-Chief to come to Nantong. 600 soldiers who have been issued return-to-unit certificates and received expenses have set off for Pukou on the Fulong ship. Local communities specially sent 1,000 catties of flatbread and 1,000 boxes of cigarettes. When the special ship set sail, military music was played and firecrackers were set off to express their farewell. The second batch will depart within five days.

Ye Kaixin Sends Personnel to Nantong to Investigate the Case: Ye Kaixin, the commander of the 8th Army, sent Yan He Jiu, the deputy director of the military department, to Nantong to investigate the case because Yan Dian Nan, a counselor of the military department, was captured in Bengbu and sent to the Zhenjiang Provincial Security Office. The investigation revealed that Yan was accused of violating the law and harming the people when he was the captain of the Nantong police team.

Provincial Security Regiment Seizes Military Supplies in the East Township: The Fourth Battalion of the Provincial Security Regiment cracked down on the bandit army's organization in Xi Hejia Yuan, East Township, killing five bandits. In the dungeon, they seized a total of 39 rifles and box cannons, and more than a thousand rounds of ammunition.

Cotton Picking Problem in Huainan Reclamation Area: In the Huainan and Yanfu reclamation areas, the bandit forces are rampant. Shen Guanxi, the bandit leader, openly led bandits to the cotton fields to pick cotton. Representatives of various companies gathered in Nantong and decided to request Xiong Yang He, the police captain of Funing County, to temporarily compile 200 police officers and follow Director Li Ming Yang's team to go to the reclamation area to pick cotton.

Rugao

Juegang Pirates Rampant: On the night of the 24th, a pirate ship suddenly came to Beikan Port in Juegang, with more than ten pirates on board. They broke into the home of Chen Jinliang, who was engaged in salt burning, first searched the place, and then tied up and kidnapped three people, including the son of Shi Wang and his son-in-law Yao Si Hou. After the pirates robbed the family, they went to the home of Cai Weichang nearby and broke down the door. Cai knew the pirates were coming and escaped through the back door, avoiding misfortune. Seeing that the people had escaped, the bandits destroyed all the belongings in the house. Two bundles in the room were carried away by the bandits. At 5:00 am on the 25th, armed bandits landed from a ship in Beikan Port. Bai Yuntao, the captain of the Dayu Town Special Task Force of the Juegang District Defense Corps, led a team to rush there. When the team arrived in Beikan, the bandits had already reached the 13th Zong area. Captain Bai caught up and opened fire with the bandits. The two sides fought fiercely. As a result, a bandit squad leader, Liu La Qian (from Yancheng), was killed, along with several other bandits. One bandit was captured alive. The corps soldiers used a broadsword to chop off the head and display it to the public. The remaining bandits fled.

Fugitive Criminals Attempt to Escape and are Killed: Chen, the captain of the First Squad of the First Company of the Juegang District Defense Corps in this county, which is stationed at the Zhou Family Ancestral Hall in Xia Man Zao, captured a man named Huang Bai Tai yesterday in the area and took him back to the team headquarters. Unexpectedly, on the way, the bandit tried to escape and was killed.

Yangzhou

Bao Long Crashes into Da Hu Ferry: The Da Da Hu ferry entered Guazhou Port at 8:00 am on the first day. Suddenly, the sound of a steam whistle was heard and the Da Hu ferry stopped to give way. Unexpectedly, the Li Tong Bao Long, which was following behind, entered the port at full speed and crashed into the waist of the Da Hu ferry. The passengers of the Da Hu ferry were in an uproar for a time and clashed with each other, fortunately no one was in danger. It is now reported that Da Hu has filed a lawsuit with the competent authorities.

Zhenjiang

County Magistrate Su Starts Military Training: The Jiangsu Provincial Government, upon receiving an order from the Ministry of the Interior, established a training institute for local administrative personnel in the province, first providing military training to qualified county magistrates who have passed the examination. The institute is now ready for operation. The site is located at the former Qianqiuqiao Garrison Office. Chairman Ye concurrently serves as the director, Jin Tiqian is responsible for academic affairs, and Yang Fangzhen is responsible for administrative affairs. Shen Zhen and Wang Zhongyue are invited to serve as military instructors. In addition to military subjects being emphasized in the entire curriculum, totaling three hours each day, the next important subjects are Party Doctrine, and the province's laws and regulations. Provincial government committee members take turns giving lectures on the actual administrative situation at the institute every day. The opening ceremony was held at 8:00 am yesterday morning, attended by twenty-six students. The ceremony was held as scheduled. Chairman Ye first gave a report, roughly stating that recently in the province, because the central government has focused all its efforts on suppressing the rebellion, it has had to take measures to deal with the bandits and reactionary forces in various counties. However, the more it deals with them, the more rampant they become. When the military affairs of suppressing the rebellion are over, it will inevitably have to plan to eliminate them. Therefore, when the central government's military affairs end, the province's military affairs will begin. Subsequently, Yang Xing Qin, a member of the Provincial Party Department, and Sun Hong Zhe and He Yu Shu, members of the Provincial Government, gave successive speeches. Finally, Li Jin Fang, the representative of the students, replied. After the ceremony, a photo was taken.

Chuansha

Handover Between New and Old County Magistrates: Ruan Kai Ji, the magistrate of Chuansha County, has been in office for two years. On September 28, he received an order from the provincial government to be transferred to Huaiyin County as magistrate, and the vacancy was filled by Tu Guang Jun. After receiving the order, Magistrate Ruan immediately ordered the sections to rush to complete the handover. The new county magistrate, Tu Guang Jun, arrived in Chuansha by boat at 3:00 pm on the first day and visited Magistrate Ruan at the county government to discuss everything. He took over the county on the second day at 10:00 am.

Gaoyou

Teachers and Staff Demand Salary for the Fifth Time: The teachers and staff of various schools in the urban area of this county are currently demanding the salary owed by the Education Bureau, but have not received any results. Yesterday afternoon, all the teachers and staff unanimously resigned to their respective principals and distributed a resignation declaration along the street. This morning (the 29th), they invited the principals to go to the Education Bureau together to demand their salary.

Qingjiang

Strangulation of an Unfilial Parricide: Yin Feng Xiang, a resident of Xiba in Huaiyin, had been gambling and losing money, and repeatedly asked his mother for money to pay off his debts, but to no avail. Suddenly, in May or June of this year, when he was drunk, he asked his mother for money again, but she still refused to give it to him. Feng Xiang suddenly had the idea of killing his mother, and used a hoe to cut off his mother's nasal bridge, causing serious injuries that led to her death. Fearing implication, the neighbors handed Yin Feng Xiang over to the Third District Office, which was submitted to the county by Chen Pin Zhi Junchen. After several interrogations, Feng Xiang confessed to killing his mother without denying it. After the county government summoned Yin's neighbors to prove that it was correct, it sent a telegram to the Provincial Government's Department of Civil Affairs for approval, and sentenced him to strangulation. This afternoon (the 29th), the county government sent police to tie up and escort the unfilial parricide Yin Feng Xiang to the execution ground outside the West Gate to carry out the strangulation.

Breakthrough in the Yun Tong Small Ferry Robbery Case: The Tong Yun small ferry from Yang Zhuang to Suqian in Huaiyin was robbed by bandits when it arrived in Zhang Zhuang area in the second district of Suqian some days ago, and eight hostages were taken. Later, after strict investigation by District Chief Jiang of the first district, the hostage Liu Ming Yi and the stolen money, silver dollars, and banknotes were completely copied out. The bandits Cao Jia Kuan, Zhang You Quan, Zhang Fang Bao, Lu Xian Di, and Wu Zhang Shi and other five people were arrested and sent to the county for handling.

Fengxian

The Adjudicator Firmly Resigned: The adjudicator Zhou Xiang has recently resigned to the High Court because the handling of affairs has been thorny, and there have been many accusations against the handling of escaped prisoners. Today, he came to Nanfeng, handled the more than fifty unsettled cases separately, and decided to leave Fengxian immediately to show his determination.

Poor Woman Forced to Drown Herself and Rescued: Jin Fei, a farmer in the 17th Tu of the Fifth District, previously filed a lawsuit with the county, accusing Yu Meifang, a wealthy household in the area, of oppressing poor tenants and swallowing mortgage rents. After being filed five times, Yu hid in Shanghai and refused to confront her, causing the woman to go back and forth in vain and the case was suspended. Yesterday was the hearing date, and because the defendant did not arrive, no joint interrogation was conducted. On the way back, the woman encountered a thunderstorm and was drenched. Overwhelmed with resentment and anger, she threw herself into the river in an attempt to commit suicide. Fortunately, a passerby saw her and rescued her, avoiding an accident. Now, after hearing about it, the county has sent police officers to Shanghai to arrest Yu and investigate the case.

Shaoxing

Petition to Postpone the Handling of Zha Gate Land Tax: Huang, the magistrate of Shaoxing, and Ling, the director of the Finance Bureau, stated that the upper busy land tax to offset gold this year has been levied since July 1. According to regulations, those who have not completed payment should be penalized from October 1. Now, because the counties and towns in the county have suffered from disasters and poor harvests for many years, and the people's strength is insufficient, they specially petitioned the provincial departments yesterday to postpone the penalty for one month.

Ordered to Collect Additional Tax on Parcel Post: The Shaoxing Unified Tax Bureau has been ordered by the province to have the Unified Tax Bureau continue to collect the additional tax on parcel post collected by the Postal Tax Bureau and the Zhejiang West Water Conservancy funds according to the previous method. Director Yuan is now in contact with the Postal Tax Bureau and will send personnel to the Postal Tax Bureau's collection office to collect the tax at the same time starting from October 1, and stamp the postal tax票 separately as proof.

Jiaxing

Bandit Suppression Headquarters Executes Five Kidnappers: Jiang Lai Sheng, a kiln owner in Xiadianmiao, a place where Jiaxing and Jiashan intersect, was kidnapped by bandits on September 21. Later, Sun Feng Chi, the captain of the 8th Water Police Team, dispatched detectives to conduct a strict investigation, and learned that Shen Mao, who secretly sold lamps and opium in Xiadianmiao, was harboring bandits. He arrested Shen and interrogated him, and learned that Yang Shi Sheng was quite suspicious. Then, he arrested Yang and interrogated him, and learned that the case was initiated by Shao Zhong Xian and Shen Mao, and they had sent a letter to Jiang's family, agreeing to contact them at the Jiashen East Gate machine oil car on September 26. After obtaining the confession, Captain Sun sent detectives to guard the oil car and arrested the bandit Shao Jin Ming. Shao also confessed the location where the hostage was hidden. The detectives then took Shao Jin Ming to Shao's house in Qianzhuang and rescued the hostage Jiang Lai Sheng. They also captured two bandits, Shao Zhong Xian and Wu A Xiao, and seized a handgun. They were all taken back to the team headquarters for interrogation. After interrogation, the five kidnappers who were arrested one after another were escorted to the 2nd District of the Water Police and then to the Jiahu Bandit Suppression Headquarters for interrogation. They confessed to the kidnapping and were identified by the hostage Jiang Lai Sheng as being true. Commander Hang immediately sentenced them to death in accordance with the regulations for punishing bandits. The five bandits, Shen Mao Er, Shao Zhong Xian, Shao Jin Ming, Yang Bao Sheng, and Wu A Xiao, were escorted to the scene of the crime in Xiadianmiao the day before yesterday and executed by shooting.

Pinghu

Fang Li Sentenced to Six Months of Imprisonment: Fang Li, the former magistrate of Pinghu County, was impeached for dereliction of duty and malfeasance. He was ordered by the Department of Civil Affairs to be dismissed and sent to the Hangzhou County Local Court for legal punishment. It is now learned that the case has been clearly investigated by the prosecutor of the Criminal Court, and a public prosecution has been filed. Judge Chen Huamin has held two court sessions to summon and interrogate them. The accountants of Fang Huiyuan and others have all confessed that the expenditure of public funds was all Fang Li's idea. Then the defense was declared over. Yesterday, after interrogation, he was sentenced to six months of imprisonment.

Two Cases of Embezzlement and Escape: Wanhe Xie Rice Store, located at the foot of Lv Gong Bridge outside the East Gate, has always been known for its prudence. Yesterday was the deadline for settling accounts with the stores in the urban area, but Wang took 600 yuan from a certain money house without authorization, due to the huge amount of credit owed and the fact that the salary in the line has also been paid. Qian Zhuang ran away without a trace. Ju Jingsi, an apprentice at Gantai Gong Rice Store outside the West Gate, asked his store to carry 350 yuan yesterday and handed it over to the bank for safekeeping. Check as the Yellow Crane, and never return.

Xiaoshan

Provincial Committee Re-investigates Abuses in Tooth Certificates: The tooth certificates of various tooth companies in Xiaoshan were previously ordered to be promoted to higher grades. A Provincial Committee member, Yuan Ming Chang, was sent to investigate each household. Later, because the provincial government believed that the committee member had collected improper fees when investigating the tooth certificates, he was dismissed immediately after being reported. The county government was ordered to transfer the improper fees collected by Yuan to the Chamber of Commerce and investigate each industry clearly, issue the money to the rightful owners, and re-dispatch committee member Yan Le Tian for a re-investigation. It is now known that Committee Member Yan arrived in Xiaoshan yesterday (the 27th) and set off for a household-by-household investigation.

Special Article

Kamal's Design Committee of the Ministry of Finance 76

Opinion on Tax Revenue Policy

Preface: If the Chinese government today wants to seek development in the income aspect of financial construction, it is better to proceed cautiously with the improvement of existing tax sources, and should not easily try to open up new paths. The progress of China's financial administration gives us a major reason for this conclusion. Except for customs and salt affairs, China's tax administration has been inefficient and supervision has been improper. No generally recognized procedural regulations have been seen, nor have there been satisfactory tax standards. Taxpayers do not know that taxes are used to maintain various public services, and even ordinary rulers may not be able to truly understand this meaning. The above is all a past fact, with no praise or derogation in it.

The purpose of taxation is to seek public interest, not to take advantage of the people's property by the government or to be filled by officials' pockets. However, in order to make the people understand this concept of taxation, public funds must be used for public utilities, such as schools, public health, roads, and the suppression of bandits and other illegal acts, and should not be used for civil war and affairs that have little to do with the public, or for the salaries of redundant personnel. Taxpayers will gradually understand the proper meaning of taxation, and tax collectors will gradually recognize the effect of this concept, and gradually develop administrative efficiency procedures and standards. Although this progress cannot be achieved overnight, it will be successful if a tax plan suitable for China's special conditions is adopted.

In fact, financial officials of all countries are painstakingly anxious, spending years to solve the problem of offsetting revenue and expenditure. The right tax is the first principle of taxation, that is, the first requirement of the tax system. As if the financial officers are eager to pay, to make up for the loopholes, and ignore the proper development of the national tax revenue problem, and even hold prejudices, not knowing whether the tax revenue is appropriate or not depends entirely on the method of the tax system and its operation method. To seek revenue for the government, we should first measure the burden of taxpayers, and should not impose too heavy a burden on domestic industries, otherwise, it will only make the country's financial resources exhausted, which is no different from drinking poison to quench thirst. Trade and taxation: In the past, the taxes of European and Western countries were mostly the changes of the feudal system. Not only were taxes levied on land or its products, but also various transit taxes and market taxes were levied on business and trade in addition to customs duties. After the development of trade, new goods were put on the market, and the amount of tax revenue also increased accordingly to make up for the increasing expenditure. Therefore, the scope of taxation became increasingly expanded, and as a result of most of the daily activities of human society, there was an obligation to pay taxes.

In modern times, all countries have a tendency to concentrate on a few sources of finance. They know that excessive taxation is enough to hinder the development of society and damage the interests of the national treasury. On the contrary, taxing only a few special items not only saves the cost of collection, but also the tax rate can be higher.

At present, there are still many items of tax in China, which are all ancient systems and have not been reformed since the overthrow of the Manchu Qing Dynasty. Furthermore, because the political and military problems are unresolved, the fiscal officers are only busy with the amount of tax revenue and have no time to take care of the reform of taxation, and make the financial relationship between the central and local governments chaotic. Therefore, there is no way to build administrative supervision that can rely on reforming tax revenue.

The new tax policy of China should first aim at reducing the types of tax. In addition, the repeated taxes levied on the same goods must be removed. Many commodities often increase their costs due to repeated taxation, so that no profit can be obtained when sold.

The most important result of reducing the types of taxes and repeated collection will be to release the general trade from the shackles of heavy taxes. It must be known that such shackles can reduce the total amount of trade, limit the profits obtained by merchants in their operations, and cause harm to the whole country. If the existing shackles are removed one by one, the national income will inevitably increase significantly due to the prosperity of the enterprise and the increase of taxed goods. The precedents of European and Western countries can be believed to be inevitable.

The most harmful tax to commerce and its prosperity in Chinese taxation is lijin. The committee has discussed the lijin system and raised considerable opinions. If the committee's recommendations can be followed, the lijin system can be gradually abolished, and other taxes similar in nature to lijin should also be abolished. The most notable of these are Changguan 税, Fukun Ren 税, and Chinese ports reciprocal taxes. (To be continued)

Important News

Restoration of Education in Hunan Province 77

丨Schools to Reopen on October 1st丨

University President Not in Hunan

Students Fearful, Initiate Reading Movement

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province, having fallen to the Gui Army on June 3rd and then to the Communist bandits on July 27th, suffered extensive losses, both public and private. In particular, during the Communist occupation, in addition to plundering property, they engaged in indiscriminate burning and killing, paying special attention to educational institutions. Consequently, the Education Commissioner's Office and the Provincial Education Advancement Hall were both burned down. Taking the losses of the Provincial Education Association alone, the Zhongshan Hall building was valued at 145,500 silver dollars, the magic lantern theater at 48,780 silver dollars, the museum building at 45,000 silver dollars, equipment costs at approximately one million silver dollars, the library building at 60,000 silver dollars, books and equipment at 926,000 silver dollars, the office building at 14,920 silver dollars, the Cixian Garden building at 1,500 silver dollars, association equipment and documents at 38,125 silver dollars, and staff luggage and books at 985 silver dollars. In total, excluding the priceless ancient bronzes in the museum and rare books in the library, the estimated loss amounts to 2,280,810 silver dollars. The extent of other losses remains unknown. He Jian, after recovering Changsha, faced empty coffers and insufficient tax revenue due to high military expenses. Therefore, he temporarily borrowed educational funds. With the Communist bandits not completely suppressed and many schools damaged, the government initially planned to suspend all provincial schools this semester. However, figures in the education sector, considering education the foundation of the nation and vital to the future, repeatedly convened meetings. Private schools were to be prepared by their respective responsible parties to ensure classes could resume and maintain the status quo. Regarding provincial schools, a joint petition was submitted, urging that a way be found to operate them despite the difficulties. The Education Department presented this to the Provincial Government Committee, which unanimously agreed that students should not be deprived of their education and that educators were willing to endure hardship together. Their enthusiasm for maintaining education was highly commendable and should be supported. It was decided that all provincial schools would uniformly reopen on October 1st. However, due to current economic difficulties, only 50% of the October funds would be temporarily issued for reopening purposes. The school principals, since the government would not suspend operations, were largely willing to manage as best they could. They are now successively receiving funds and actively preparing. Hunan University, No. 1 Middle School, No. 1 Vocational School, and others have already announced that classes will begin on October 4th or 5th. The names of the principals of the provincial schools are listed below: Hunan University - Hu Yuantan, No. 1 Middle School - Miao Yunan, No. 2 Middle School - Wang Chengshu, No. 3 Middle School - Zhang [missing character], No. 4 Middle School - Li Wenying, No. 5 Middle School - Tang Jie, No. 6 Middle School - Liu Zhiyuan, No. 1 Vocational School - Cheng Xiwem, No. 1 Agricultural School - Ming Xun, No. 1 Normal School - Xie Zhen, No. 1 Vocational School - Zhou Fenggu, No. 2 Vocational School - Hu Shanzhi, No. 3 Vocational School - Hu Shikun, No. 4 Vocational School - Tan Bin, No. 6 Vocational School - Luo Baozhen, No. 8 Vocational School - Wu Shaolin, No. 2 Women's Vocational School - Miao Guojun.

Changsha Correspondence: Through the efforts of educational figures in Hunan Province, all provincial schools have been scheduled to reopen on October 1st, with classes beginning on the 4th and 5th. However, Hu Yuantan, the president of Hunan University, is currently not in Hunan. Although he has entrusted the school affairs to Yang Zhuoxin as acting president, he has also submitted a request to the provincial government to resign from his position as president. Yang states that because only 50% of the funding has been received and many faculty members have scattered, managing everything is extremely difficult. Therefore, he declares that he will be responsible only until October 5th and will not be involved in whether classes resume thereafter. The students, surprised that the president is firmly resigning and the acting president will no longer be responsible after repeated requests for the school to be allowed to operate, held a general meeting of students in the province today. Over 300 people attended. He Qianyuan chaired the meeting, reported on the purpose of the meeting and the school's situation. After discussion, the following was unanimously decided: (1) To organize a temporary student representative assembly of Hunan University to actively promote a reading movement. (2) To telegraph President Hu, urging him to reconsider his resignation and return to the school as soon as possible to take charge of everything. (3) To telegraph the Dean of the Engineering School, Liu Kezhun, the Director of Affairs, Tang Yiqing, the Auditing Director, Yi Ganqiu, and all faculty members who have left the province, urging them to return to Hunan as soon as possible. (4) To submit a request to the Provincial Government to telegraph President Hu, urging him to return to the school, and to allocate funds to maintain the school's operations. (5) To submit a request to the Provincial Government to order the people and troops stationed in Pingliu Beach to vacate the school. (6) To write to President Yang Zhuoxin, asking him to consider the students' studies and maintain the school's affairs until President Hu returns. (7) To notify students in all counties to come to the school immediately. (8) All students in the province will move into the school before October 1st to facilitate the start of classes as scheduled. The meeting adjourned after making these decisions.

Implementation Outline for the Popular Education Experiment Zone of the Jiangsu Yijiao Office 78

The implementation outline for the popular education experiment zone (Zhongleng New Village) of the Jiangsu Province's County Preparatory Compulsory Education Joint Office has been revised by the Joint Office as follows: (1) The purpose of this zone is to use the power of education to develop the economy, improve the organization, and promote the culture of the entire zone, thereby creating Zhongleng New Village and establishing a model for a new popular education plan. (2) The implementation policy is to treat the entire community as a school, the people as students, and the improvement of the entire life of the people as education. (3) The pre-determined specific goals are: A. Economic aspects, divided into eight items; B. Political aspects, divided into nine items; C. Cultural aspects, divided into six items. (4) The pre-planned undertakings are: 1. Organize the Zhongleng New Village Preparatory Committee; 2. Establish a community park; 3. Open an agricultural experiment field; 4. Organize an irrigation cooperative; 5. Develop a natural park; 6. Promote compulsory education; 7. Implement adult literacy education; 8. Contract farmland. (5) The organizational structure includes a design committee and a preparatory committee, which is divided into three sections: executive, livelihood autonomy, and culture. The research section is divided into three groups: survey, planning, and compilation. The administrative section is divided into three groups: documentation, general affairs, and accounting. (6) The implementation process is as follows: Phase 1: August 19th to January 20th - Select the zone site, determine the implementation outline, conduct a zone survey, organize the Zhongleng New Village Preparatory Committee, establish a community park, organize an irrigation cooperative, establish an agricultural experiment field, and establish a phonetic symbol training center. Phase 2: February 20th to July - Open community schools, establish contracted farmland, promote fish farming, develop a natural park, establish model families, establish a music association, prepare for a childcare center, conduct a health campaign, and widely establish compulsory schools. Phase 3: August 20th to January 21st - Organize a youth league and a women's association, establish a library, and establish a fire brigade. Phase 4: February 21st to July - Determine the path for developing the zone's livelihood, report on simple methods for promoting popular education, and establish various social education enterprises, popularize methods for community recreation, and develop local autonomy. Phase 5: August 21st to January 22nd - Education is universal, social institutions are complete, the people's livelihood is prosperous, local autonomy is complete, and a beautiful environment is created. The above is part of the planned implementation outline for the experiment zone. Additions and subtractions to undertakings and changes in order will be determined separately on a temporary basis during implementation.

Local News

Declaration of the Labor University School Affairs Meeting 81

Narrating President Yi's achievements... Hoping the successor will be a suitable person. The other day, the National Labor University School Affairs Meeting discussed the matter of President Yi's inability to concurrently hold the position of government official and university president and resolved to issue a declaration. The full text of the declaration is as follows:

Our school was founded three years ago and has a special purpose among national universities, and a special mission in the process of the Three Principles of the People's National Revolution. This meeting, in order to implement the special purpose of our school and complete the special mission of our school, should at any time publicize the purpose and mission to the society in order to arouse the attention and sympathy of the national education community and even the general public, and promote the development of our school's future. Therefore, we cannot help but contribute a word to society.

The spirit of modern education lies in adapting to the trends of the times and the needs of the nation. The trend of the times is the expression of the demands of the times, and the needs of the nation are the key to national problems. Today, the era in which China is located is the era of the liberation of laborers. The need of the Chinese nation is to awaken the laboring masses, participate in the national revolution, and strive for the free and equal status of the entire nation. Therefore, the purpose of our school is to experiment with labor education and develop labor education in order to increase the knowledge of laborers and achieve the goal of liberating laborers. The Chinese National Revolution opened a new era in Chinese history, and labor education opened a new era in Chinese education. If we can focus on the relationship between education and the trends of the times and the needs of the nation, and also understand the current situation in China, we should not be shocked by the special purpose of our school, and we should have the enthusiasm to maintain this only labor education institution in the country. The founding of our school was in the autumn of 1927, when the Chinese revolution was at its height, inspiring the whole country. The revolutionary government was laying the foundation in the southeast, and the advanced figures of the party and the country first focused on the establishment of the highest labor education institution in the midst of military affairs. The revolutionary government also took the establishment of the Labor University as the first step in refreshing education. Our school came into being in response to the development of the Chinese revolution, opening the first chapter of education in the revolutionary era. We originally wanted to set an example, inspiring the whole country to promote the revolution with labor education and realize the liberation of laborers. This is our aim.

In the three years since our school was founded, we cannot but express our deep respect and gratitude to Mr. Yi Peiji, the founder and first president, for the difficulty of the construction. President Yi was entrusted by the government with the important task of starting from scratch. At the beginning of the preparation, everything was in its infancy. School buildings were to be sought, scale was to be built, and regulations were to be drafted. As the ancient saying goes (carving out a path in the mountains with simple tools). The difficult management can be generally seen. In the three years, we have also encountered turbulent times and financial difficulties. For the sake of the development of our school, on the one hand, we must seek the expansion of construction and equipment, and on the other hand, we must consider the accommodation of the youth in the school. Today, our school has completed the establishment of the School of Engineering, the School of Agriculture, the School of Social Sciences, and the Middle School and Primary School. It accommodates more than a thousand poor and ambitious young people, most of whom are the elites of the children of workers and peasants. They gather together, working with their minds and bodies. The foundation of the ideal Labor University is ready, and the development is infinite. President Yi has been engaged in education for many years and has accumulated rich experience and honors. Therefore, he has been able to administer the school with the eyes of an educator, adhering to impartiality, sincerity, and leadership. Now our school has clear and orderly regulations and a simple and enterprising academic style. All of these are the achievements of President Mao in presiding over our school, which will forever be a model for future generations. The colleagues of this meeting hope that the school authorities who founded the Labor University can implement the purpose and expand the enterprise. Unexpectedly, President Yi could not get rid of the position of president because of the example of being unable to hold concurrent positions. We deeply regret that we could not retain him. Now we only express our sincere wish, hoping that President Yi will continue to maintain labor education with the spirit of several years of struggle and the historical relationship of the founder, so that our school can move forward. The colleagues of this meeting, standing on the educational and revolutionary positions, should also encourage each other with this.

The prerequisite for maintaining our school in the future is to hope that the successor president can obtain suitable talents. We believe that the current education authorities should be able to understand the relationship between labor education and the Chinese revolution, and should be able to treat our school as a special university. The revolutionary government established the Labor University to express the spirit of the educational policy of the revolutionary party. The education authorities should never neglect it out of anger. This meeting must determine the standard of the successor president's choice in order to prevent the wind of competition and live up to the expectations of the society. To sum up, it can be listed as follows: (1) Those who have the history and revolutionary spirit of the Chinese Kuomintang, (2) Those who understand labor education and are willing to devote themselves to the development of labor education, (3) Those who have considerable achievements in running university education, (4) Those who can continue the existing scale of our school and strive for development, (5) Those who can concentrate on their work and not hold concurrent positions, (6) Those who have high moral character and profound learning, (7) Those who have a global perspective. The above articles are all aimed at selecting talents for the special purpose of our school, hoping that the education authorities will pay attention to it and carefully select the person. Only in this way can the successor be able to continue the previous work and expect development. Furthermore, the key to maintaining labor education in the future is to determine the status of our school as a special university. Our school aims to experiment with labor education and develop labor education, and it should be determined as a special university, this is the first. Our school enrolls poor and ambitious young people and provides free education. In today's society, when the economy is frequently threatened, it has become a major issue in national education to help poor and out-of-school young people. Our school has been able to shoulder this responsibility and should be determined as a special university, this is the second. Our school students carry out physical work while studying advanced academics. The talents trained in the future will have advanced knowledge and will be able to operate with the laboring masses. They are special talents needed for the Chinese revolution and should be determined as a special university, this is the third. In short, the purpose of our school's education is to absorb poor and ambitious young people and train them to become leading talents in labor education in order to adapt to the requirements of the Chinese National Revolution today and the requirements of production. The status of a special university can never be shaken. Our school follows the university regulations and various laws and regulations in its regulations, curriculum, and equipment. Although its history is very short among national universities, its scale is complete and its achievements are obvious. This meeting has the responsibility to maintain our school. For all attempts to destroy our university, we will adhere to justice, be unyielding, and fight resolutely. We hope that the national education community and the general public who are enthusiastic about labor education will express their sympathy. Not only will the thousands of young people in the whole school benefit from it, but the future of Chinese labor education will also have unlimited development. September 24, 1920.

World Baseball Championship 86

First Day: Asia Team Wins 5-2 Against Canada Team

丨President Hoover Throws the First Pitch丨

(Philadelphia, 1st - Electric News Agency) - This year's World Series, between the National League champion, the St. Louis Cardinals (hereinafter referred to as the Canada Team), and the American League champion, the Philadelphia Athletics (hereinafter referred to as the Asia Team), began at 1:33 PM on the 1st at Shibe Park in Philadelphia after President Hoover threw the first pitch. The weather was clear and crisp, perfect for sports. 35,000 spectators flocked to the stands in the morning. In the beginning, both sides fought bravely and did not give way. The Asia Team scored first in the second inning, and the Canada Team scored two points in one fell swoop in the third inning, reversing the situation. The Asia Team scored another point in the fourth inning, tying the game. Afterwards, the Asia Team scored one point each in the sixth, seventh, and eighth innings, resulting in a 5-2 victory for the Asia Team. Although the Canada Team recorded nine hits, they only scored two points due to the skillful judgment of the Asia Team pitcher, Gulapp. Although the Asia Team only recorded five hits, they scored two home runs, so they were able to win easily. The game ended at 3:30 PM. The game progress:

First inning: No score for both teams (Canada 0, Asia 0).

Second inning: Asia Team scores first (Canada 0, Asia 1).

Third inning: Canada Team's Mangaso records a hit, then Kirbardu also records a hit. Grimes then lightly hits a ball, taking advantage of the enemy's confusion to succeed, getting a good opportunity with bases loaded and no outs. Adams hits a sacrifice fly to center field, and the base runner scores, making it a tie. Adams hits another sacrifice fly, and Kirbardu scores, adding another point (Canada 2, Asia 0).

Fourth inning: Asia Team's Siemens hits a home run, scoring one point. Although two players on the Canada Team got on base, Grimes's three outs ended the inning (Canada 0, Asia 1).

Fifth inning: No score for both teams (Canada 0, Asia 0).

Sixth inning: Canada Team fails to get on base. After one out for the Asia Team, Pi Shengpu gets on base with three balls, and Tagus records a double, and Pi scores, adding another point (Canada 0, Asia 2).

Seventh inning: Although the Canada Team recorded two hits, nothing came of it. After one out for the Asia Team, Haas records a triple, goes past first base, and Burr's sacrifice fly allows Haas to score, adding one point (Canada 0, Asia 1).

Eighth inning: Although the Canada Team fought bravely, they could not succeed because of the Asia Team's effective defense. After two outs for the Asia Team, Gugulin flies a straight ball into a home run, adding another point (Canada 0, Asia 1).

Ninth inning: Three players on the Canada Team fail to get on base (Canada 0).

Shanghai Lawn Tennis Club B Group Singles 87

Yu Tianguang Wins Right to Final

Defeated Westerner, Hoss, Yesterday by 3 to 1

In the B Group singles championship of the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Club, our country's Yu Tianguang played against Hoss in the semi-finals at the China Tennis Court yesterday. It started at 1:30 PM. The wind was very strong and the ball's direction was unstable, making it quite difficult to play. Yu Tianguang lost the first set 4-6, but then played cautiously and attacked hard, finally winning three consecutive sets 7-5, 6-4, 6-3, reversing the situation and winning the right to the final by 3-1.

Yesterday's Chinese Singles Tennis: Sun Wins Against Guo 88

Liu and Sun to Face Off in Today's Semi-Finals

The Chinese Singles Tennis Championship held two matches yesterday. The first was a semi-final between Sun Chengbi and Shao Leping, which Sun won 6-3, 1-6, 6-0, 6-3, earning a spot in the finals. The second was a semi-final between Guo Qida and Qian Wenbao, a fierce five-set battle with the following results:

Guo Qida: 6-1, 3-6, 6-4, 2-6, 6-3 defeated Qian Wenbao

Guo and Qian began their match at 3:30 PM and played until around 6:00 PM, when the city's lights were already on, before finally ending the game. Guo's 3-2 victory shows how intense their competition was. Their skills were evenly matched, requiring twenty or thirty rallies to determine each point. Both were equally determined, like chewing gum stuck to each other, refusing to let go. By the fifth set, both were exhausted, but Guo ultimately won 6-3 in a final struggle. It is said that Qian Wenbao manages a tennis court for a tennis association in this city (i.e., makes a living as a tennis partner), and should not have been allowed to participate in this competition, due to oversight.

Additionally, Liu Keng and Sun Chengbi will hold a semi-final match at the China Tennis Court at 3:30 PM today.

Circulation of Domestic Rice 93

Fundamental Measures to Prohibit Rice Exports and Crack Down on Speculation

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Submits to the Municipal Government to Forward to the Central Government

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, according to the report of the Municipal Food Commission, states that the ban on the export of Zhejiang rice has resulted in rice prices lower than those in Shanghai, making it difficult for farmers to sell their new rice at good prices, leading to disappointment. Furthermore, since Jiangsu and Zhejiang are intertwined, circulation is especially important. The government is requested to reaffirm the ban on speculation, but strictly prohibit private exports to ensure food for all. The bureau believes that the circulation of domestic rice has already been ordered by the government. This time, the

Page 10

Third Edition 94

Zhejiang province's ban on rice exports is likely due to the fact that Zhejiang rice has always been insufficient to meet demand. Leaving a surplus can compensate for the shortage. Furthermore, there is a fear that after export, rice will be smuggled abroad. However, if each province issues bans, it will inevitably lose the benefits of circulation. Farmers are eager to sell, goods suffer from congestion, and merchants take advantage of the situation to depreciate the value. Although there is an actual harvest, the income of farmers is no different from a famine year. Therefore, for the current plan to maintain the people's food supply, the only thing to do is to jointly strictly enforce the maritime ban to prevent smuggling. If rice prices fall due to closed borders, it is feared that cunning merchants will come up with all kinds of tricks. If the maritime ban is slightly relaxed, smuggling will inevitably occur, and the situation will become more complicated, making it difficult to achieve the intended goal. Therefore, the Municipal Government is requested to forward to the Executive Yuan, reaffirming the ban on speculation and strictly ordering customs officials to prevent smuggling in order to prevent unscrupulous merchants from smuggling rice abroad.

Money Industry Announces Advance Notice of Year-End Closing 95

The money industry's year-end closing, which was hurried last year, did not allow enough time for preparation. The government was petitioned to allow for flexible arrangements. This year, it will be impossible to continue in this manner. The Money Industry Association resolved the matter a few days ago. The year-end closing is imperative and should be announced to fellow traders and all business associates in advance. At the same time, letters should be sent to out-of-town business contacts to ensure consistency. The notice is recorded as follows:

Circular Letter from the Shanghai Money Industry Association Regarding the Year-End Closing. Letters were sent to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and other organizations yesterday. The letter states: Greetings. Our colleagues have long complied with the adoption of the Gregorian calendar. Year-end closing is a major conclusion for the business community. Except for pre-ordered futures, all receivables and payables must be cleared at this time in order to fulfill the final accounts and determine the profit and loss for the year. At the end of last year, due to the initial adoption of the Gregorian calendar, there was insufficient preparation, and the government allowed a one-month extension. Now that the Gregorian calendar has been adopted for the year-end closing, it should naturally be carried out at the end of the Gregorian calendar year without any doubt. However, it has been heard that there are still many merchants in the mainland who are still using the lunar calendar. Shanghai is the hub of commerce, and the money industry has the responsibility of financial circulation. Usually, businesses release goods, whether in cash or in goods, and must go from A to B to C, endlessly. By the end of the year, C pays to B, and B returns to A, and its conclusion lies in the financial industry. If the year-end closing of the Gregorian calendar this year cannot be concluded as scheduled due to the habits of various places, there is a great danger. After convening our colleagues for detailed discussions, it was unanimously agreed that the year-end closing should comply with the Gregorian calendar as a matter of course. Now that the end of the Gregorian calendar year is still far away, a notice should be published in the newspaper in advance, and the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce should be requested to notify businesses nationwide, and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce should send letters to various industries, so that the year-end closing of the Gregorian calendar will not be hindered, and the Gregorian calendar can be implemented here, and businesses will not be in danger, which is very fortunate. In addition to publishing the notice in the newspaper and sending letters to various industries through the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, we hereby earnestly request your association to promptly verify and forward it, which will be greatly appreciated.

Notice from the Money Industry Association to Fellow Traders states: Greetings. The government has strictly ordered the implementation of the Gregorian calendar year-end closing this year, and our colleagues should comply. All receivables and payables should be closed at the end of the Gregorian calendar year. Fearing that this has not been fully communicated, we are publishing this notice in the newspaper in advance. We hope you will take note. The Money Industry Association.

Sino-Japanese Telecommunications Negotiations 96

No Definite Date for Continued Discussions

After the temporary suspension of the third Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiation, the Japanese committee members have telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for instructions on the revision of the Nagasaki-Shanghai line treaty. Before receiving a reply from the Japanese government, it will be difficult to hold a meeting to negotiate. Therefore, the third meeting still does not have a definite date. However, our committee members have already made arrangements for the opening procedures of the three meetings, so they are waiting for a definite response from the Japanese side these days. Japanese Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu Aoi, in order to ensure the smooth progress of the negotiations, has telegraphed the Japanese Consul Uemura in Beijing to exchange opinions with our committee member Zhuang Zhihuan and others in a non-official manner to eliminate misunderstandings. If the Japanese government sends instructions to Shanghai within the next few days, the Japanese committee members will be able to go to Beijing to hold a meeting soon. However, it is heard that the Japanese government attaches great importance to the Shanghai-Nagasaki sea line and is unwilling to easily sacrifice its sovereignty. Therefore, the future of the negotiations is difficult, and this line is the biggest obstacle.

The Third Day of National Anti-Drug Week 98

Promoting Anti-Drug Hygiene

Focusing on Smoking Cessation Efforts

Today is the Hygiene Day of the 7th National Anti-Drug Week. The vigorous activities of the past two days have already been reported in this newspaper. We now specially record the activities of yesterday (Law-Abiding Day) and today (Hygiene Day) as follows:

Activities of Law-Abiding Day: Yesterday was the second day of Anti-Drug Week. The purpose of the day's activities was to promote people's voluntary compliance with the law and to request the government to implement prohibition laws. The association specially (1) petitioned the National Government to abolish the special taxes of Hunan and Hubei to maintain the ban on opium and protect the country's reputation; (2) petitioned the Central Government to instruct all provinces to strictly prohibit the cultivation of opium poppies; (3) telegraphed all national groups and organizations, anti-drug groups, to report illegal officials, soil traffickers, and treacherous merchants, as well as organizations and groups, and anti-drug comrades who themselves have the habit of smoking opium, to make every effort to report them and severely punish them according to law; (4) petitioned the government to implement anti-opium laws. In addition, colorful posters and slogans for this Anti-Drug Week were posted at the entrance of the Shanghai Postal Administration and more than 20 branch offices throughout the city. They were also widely posted in the carriages of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways and at various branch stations. The Anti-Drug Association sent personnel to post them on all major roads, and each store was presented with beautiful picture slogans.

Enthusiastic Participation in Other Cities: According to preliminary reports, more than ten provinces including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Liaoning, and Fujian were preparing to hold events. Today, the association received telegrams from various places in nearby provinces stating that Anti-Drug Week activities were being held in Ningbo, Suzhou, Hangzhou, Jiaxing, Yiwu, Wujin, Nantong, Zhenjiang, Changxing, Chongde, and other places.

Central Newspaper Continuously Publishes Special Issues: Yesterday, the association received special issues from other cities, including the Jiangsheng, Ningbo Min Guo, Hangzhou Min Guo, and Wujin Zhongshan newspapers. The Nanjing Central Daily News especially praised and supported anti-drug efforts. In addition to publishing a special issue on the opening day, it also published a special issue every day for the following seven days, a total of seven issues, and the association is currently writing materials and submitting them to Beijing for use.

Municipal Party Department Issues Circular to All District Departments: The Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department issued a circular to all district party departments yesterday, requiring that anti-drug speeches and discussions be added to the memorial week held on October 6, and that party members take an anti-drug oath.

Plan for Anti-Drug Hygiene Day (A) (Significance): As the Western saying goes, a sound mind resides in a sound body. Opium, a poisonous substance, is a formidable enemy that hinders physical health, diminishes one's ambition, and turns one into a useless person once addicted. It not only reduces social production but also harms the country. Therefore, opium, a poisonous substance, is particularly closely related to personal hygiene, and all compatriots must pay attention to it. (B) (Purpose): The purpose of Anti-Drug Hygiene Day is to encourage compatriots to encourage and advise each other not to sacrifice their healthy bodies to opium, which would reduce their ability to produce and act, leading to ruin and disgrace, which would have a profound impact on society and the country. (C) (Methods): (1) Based on the association's methods, establish smoking cessation and rehabilitation centers, invite doctors from various hospitals to promote them, and ask the business community to unanimously support them and cooperate. (2) Hold smoking cessation entertainment events, invite students from various schools and public groups to join in performing new anti-drug dramas, and use the income to fund smoking cessation efforts. (3) Petition government offices to allocate funds from opium prohibition revenue to fund smoking cessation and rehabilitation centers. (4) Hold an anti-drug oath ceremony.

、　、Outline of Hygiene Day Propaganda: Weapons are not to be feared, but opium weakens the body, poisons the mind, ruins the family, and destroys the race. Imperialists strictly prohibit their own people from using it, but specialize in luring and killing people from other countries. Their intentions can be said to be extremely sinister, and the harm is ten or a hundred times greater than that of weapons. The Chinese people have been mired in a dark sea and have been weak for a long time. The "sick man of East Asia" is a disgrace. To save the people's livelihood, the first priority is to oppose drugs and promote hygiene. Let's examine the effects of opium on the human body. All four limbs and hundreds of bones are affected by the poison: (1) Nervous system: The brain and spinal cord are stimulated, cells die, and function ceases. (2) Circulatory system: Blood vessels and pulse shrink and become rapid, and blood vessels lose their ability to contract, leading to death. (3) Respiratory system: Anesthesia initially leads to excitement, but gradually extends to the respiratory center, eventually leading to paralysis and death. (4) Digestive system: Peristalsis is weak, food stagnates, and stool becomes constipated, leading to impotence, infertility, and the cessation of offspring. In terms of disease, rapid death and misdiagnosis are especially harmful: (1) The normal human body is able to avoid disease entirely through the resistance of white blood cells. Opium paralyzes white blood cells, leading to a loss of resistance and making it easy to get sick. (2) Opium addicts already have weak constitutions, and the addiction makes treatment especially difficult. (3) A disease may be curable, but the patient is deceived by the momentary anesthesia of the drug and does not seek treatment quickly, often leading to death. Therefore, the rate of death from drugs forms a terrifying proportion. According to statistics from one place in Mumbai, India, the number of children who died each year after being fed opium by female workers was as high as 66%. If adults use it to excess, the number of deaths will undoubtedly increase even more. Opium is an ominous weapon of imperialist aggression and a great enemy of mankind. For the sake of self-defense and for the sake of the people's livelihood, we must declare war on opium and never compromise. Everyone should actively rise up, actively promote, and implement the following key points of anti-drug hygiene: (1) Promote anti-drug education (add anti-drug education to the health science curriculum in schools). (2) Restrict the import of drugs (except for legitimate medical purposes). (3) Ban disguised drugs (medicines should not be sold unless they have been examined and approved). (4) Popularize anti-drug propaganda societies (the government should issue a circular to all counties across the country to uniformly advocate their establishment). (5) Promote smoking cessation efforts (all formal hospitals across the country should provide smoking cessation treatment).

Slogans: The Anti-Drug Association has produced eight slogans for use during this Anti-Drug Week. The slogans are as follows: (1) Opium is a poisonous substance that destroys the country and exterminates the race. (2) Opium and narcotic drugs are evil demons that endanger the party and the country. (3) Anti-Drug Week is a movement to awaken the masses and eliminate drugs. (4) Compatriots across the country, unite and rise up to eliminate drugs. (5) Opium and morphine are the root of ruin and bankruptcy. (6) The result of opium is family disintegration and death. (7) Anyone who plants, manufactures, transports, sells, or uses opium is a traitor. (8) If you want to strengthen the country and strengthen the race, you must first reject drugs.

Expanding the Anti-Drug Movement: The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association is taking advantage of this Anti-Drug Week to reorganize the National Anti-Drug Comrades Society into the Anti-Drug Propaganda Society and will also send personnel to the provincial, municipal, and county branches to organize them effectively in order to achieve widespread coverage. Fujian is a special opium-producing area, and the former branch had long been shut down, resulting in the increasing prevalence of opium addiction. The association specially invited enthusiastic people in the country to quickly organize and fight against it. The announcement is recorded as follows: Respectfully, our country has suffered from the scourge of opium for over a century. All people with insight are heartbroken and eager to eradicate it. Our association, entrusted by our compatriots, is working hard to carry out the anti-drug movement and will always strive to achieve complete success. It is noted that the people of Fujian have always made tireless efforts to promote the anti-drug movement. Lin Wenzhong, the anti-drug sage of your province, was enthusiastic about banning opium and ruthlessly eradicating it, which is admired by all, both ancient and modern, Chinese and foreign. Unexpectedly, in recent years, the opium scourge in Fujian Province has become increasingly rampant, and the anti-drug movement has declined. Opium seedlings are planted in counties throughout the province, and foreigners have even opened opium dens in places such as Xiamen to provide opium for people to smoke, and the harm is increasing day by day. Thinking of this, it is truly heartbreaking. As the International Opium Conference is about to be held, all of our anti-drug comrades urgently need to unite our strength, awaken the masses, and urge the government to implement the opium ban in order to save the people's livelihood and restore the lost national reputation. The opium scourge in your province is fierce, and the revival of the anti-drug movement is even more urgent. It has been found that the Fuzhou Anti-Drug Branch has been closed for a long time and there is a lack of responsible personnel. Failure to remedy this situation will be unfortunate for the future of opium prohibition. After deliberation, this meeting decided to appoint Ye Guorui, Lin Huangjuan, Sun Shihua, Ouyang Ying, Chen Guang, Zhu Yue, Weng Kan, Shen Zhizhong, Chen Hongjian, Wang Yujie, Yang Renrong, Ye Kefang, Li Zhiwen, Wang Zhaopei, and Lin Chunwang as members of the preparatory committee of the Fujian National Anti-Drug Association, and designated Ye Guorui, Zhu Chuanyue, and Shen Zhizhong as conveners. I have long known of your enthusiasm for fighting drugs and saving the country, and I hope you will work together to prepare quickly and report the progress at any time. Enclosed are the organizational outline, the anti-drug guide, and many propaganda materials. I hope you will receive and use them.

Good News from Overseas Anti-Drug Efforts: Overseas anti-drug groups have been actively promoting the anti-drug movement this year to an unprecedented extent. The association received a report from Singapore stating that the Zhenwu Charity Society of Singapore, which was restored under the promotion of Huang Jiawei, the general secretary of our association, has been established and renamed the Singapore Anti-Drug Association to match the meaning of its name. Dr. Ke Quanshou's smoking cessation method in Java has been agreed to by the local government and is being tested at the government-run Tan Tock Seng Hospital. In the future, they plan to establish their own hospital specializing in smoking cessation and are actively promoting the establishment of associations in major cities in the British colonies to build momentum.

Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau's Statement on the Public Weight Inspection of Raw Silk 99

Silk Mills' Shutdown Due to Other Reasons

Absolutely Unrelated to Public Weight Inspection

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that many silk mills in this city have stopped operations due to the weak silk market and lack of raw materials. At the same time, according to a letter from the Shanghai Silk Mill Association to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, the reason for the shutdown is the loss of points due to public weight inspection. The Xin Sheng News Agency reporter believes that the shutdown of silk mills is of great importance, and the truth behind the scenes is attracting the attention of all Shanghai residents. Yesterday afternoon, the reporter visited Zou Bingwen, director of the Commodity Inspection Bureau on Museum Road, to inquire about everything. After meeting, the reporter first stated his intention. Director Zou said that the public weight inspection of raw silk is sufficient to maintain fair trade and promote the improvement of raw silk quality and increase its value. The so-called loss of points refers to the water content that should not be in raw silk. There is no loss in the amount of real silk. Moreover, since autumn, due to the gradual dryness of the weather, the silk body has been particularly dry. As a result of the inspection, the public weight is already greater than the net weight, and there is no loss of points. All silk merchants know this very well. Therefore, the real reason for the shutdown of some silk mills this time is that Chinese silk is not selling well and there is a lack of raw materials, making it impossible to support them. Judging from the fact that the industry has been running around for this matter and calling on the government for relief, saying that more than 70% of the 106 silk mills in Shanghai have declared bankruptcy, it is sufficient to prove that the shutdown of each mill is not due to public weight inspection. The Shanghai Silk Mill Association is also well aware of this situation, but the letter still cites the loss of points due to public weight as the reason, and even said that if permission is not granted to stop, the mills will shut down and wait. The intention is extremely inexplicable. The public weight inspection of this bureau was submitted to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for approval and implementation. Without an order from the ministry, it is difficult to change it without authorization. If the merchants have reasons, they should submit them directly to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for approval, which is the proper way. This bureau has no right to decide to cancel it.

Inspection of Wheat Transported to Shanghai from the Interior 100

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asks Not to Arbitrarily Deduct Fines

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Office yesterday, stating: On the 1st of this month, according to a letter from the Shanghai Chinese Cereals, Oil Cakes, and Miscellaneous Goods Association, it was recently reported by colleagues and Yuetang that it was reported by Huaibei's resident Huojia Transfer Station from Yangzhou that the Huojia Agricultural and Mining Inspection Branch detained goods and demanded fees, and requested the Shanghai Miscellaneous Goods Association to telegraph for protection. It is noted that merchants purchase wheat and other goods in the production area and sell them in Shanghai. They are transported by private boats to Huojiaqiao, and then transported to Shanghai by Datong steamships from Huojia via Dada. Huojia is a transit point, not a production area. The government's agricultural and mining inspection is to pay attention to the improvement of agriculture, but it should strictly crack down on adulteration in the production area and the place of sale, which is the proper way. The sudden establishment of the branch in Huojiaqiao, which is neither a production area nor a place of sale, and the inspection in transit is probably not the original intention of the Agricultural and Mining Department. Recently, a fee of one cent and five liang of silver dollars is required for each bag of goods arriving in Huojia, which is not convenient to allow, resulting in detention and refusal to allow loading on the steamship. Merchants' goods are thus piled up on the Jiang'an River, and the risk is worrying. The Chamber of Commerce should be asked to maintain the telegraph and strive for exemption from inspection and release, which would be of public benefit. According to this, it is noted that Huojiaqiao is a transit area, neither a production area nor a major sales port, and it seems that there is no need to implement on-site inspection. Now that an inspection office has been set up there, it is hoped that fees will be collected for goods passing through in transit, and no effort will be spared to arbitrarily make things difficult. Goods are piled up on the Jiang'an River, and the risk is worrying. According to the previous situation, the facts are true. Therefore, a special letter is sent to Chen Junhui to quickly telegraph for restraint to facilitate commercial transportation. The aforementioned is the situation. Wheat is an agricultural product and provides food for the people. Limo absolutely protects it to facilitate circulation. Huojiaqiao is not a wheat-producing area, but an inspection branch is actually established to arbitrarily extort donations and detain goods, causing hardship for merchants and affecting the food supply in various places. It is appropriate to write to your office to inquire and request that the issuance of a prohibition be issued to facilitate passage and maintain the people's food supply to the deepest public gratitude.
